           <script>
            function showDivText(){
        divObj = document.getElementById("my-notification-button");
        var txt = divObj.textContent || divObj.innerText;
     //console.log(txt);
        if (txt == 'Unsubscribe') {
          $("#opt-btn").text('Cancel');
        } else {
            $("#opt-btn").text('Maybe later');
            }
        document.getElementsByClassName("test-container")[0].getElementsByTagName('a')[0].innerHTML=txt;  
        var permission = Notification.permission;
     //console.log(permission);
        if(permission == 'denied') {
          //console.log("Oops!!!!!!!!!!!");
            $("#promptModal").modal('hide');
            $(".dropdown-toggle").dropdown();
        } else {
            $("#promptModal").modal('show');
            $(".subscribe-dropdown-menu").hide();
        }
        
      }
           </script>

       <script>
        $(document).ready(function() {
     var userAgentValOS = getOperatingSystem();
      if (userAgentValOS == "iOS") {
        //console.log("ios");
          document.getElementById("status-btn2").style.display = "none";
      } else {
        //console.log("not ios");
          document.getElementById("status-btn2").style.display = "display: inline-block";
      }
   });
       </script>
       <script>
        function showDivText2(){
        divObj = document.getElementById("my-notification-button");
        var txt = divObj.textContent || divObj.innerText;
     //console.log(txt);
        if (txt == 'Unsubscribe') {
          $("#opt-btn").text('Cancel');
        } else {
        $("#opt-btn").text('Maybe later');
        }
        document.getElementsByClassName("test-container")[0].getElementsByTagName('a')[0].innerHTML=txt;
        var permission = Notification.permission;
     //console.log(permission);
        if(permission == 'denied') {
          //console.log("Oops!!!!!!!!!!!");
            $("#promptModal").modal('hide');
            $(".dropdown-toggle").dropdown();
        } else {
            $("#promptModal").modal('show');
            $(".dropdown-menu").hide();
        }
      }
       
   function getOperatingSystem() {
      var userAgent = navigator.userAgent || navigator.vendor || window.opera;
      // iOS detection from: http://stackoverflow.com/a/9039885/177710
      if (/(iPad|iPhone|iPod)/.test(userAgent) && !window.MSStream) {
        userAgent = "iOS";
        return userAgent;
      } else {
        userAgent = "Android";
        return userAgent;
      }
    }
       </script>

        $(document).ready(function() {
    var checkTagline = $('div.section-top-container').find("div.tagline1");
    if(checkTagline.length > 0) {      
      var childClasses = $('div.tagline1:eq(0)').attr('class');
      var splitTagArrayClasses = childClasses.split(" | ");
      var i;
      for (i = 0; i < splitTagArrayClasses.length; i++){
        var storyPosition = "";
        var tagName = "Exclusive";
        var backgroundCol = "#e71b28";
        var splitArrayClasses = splitTagArrayClasses[i].split(" ");
        if(splitArrayClasses.length>1){
          storyPosition = splitArrayClasses[1];
        }
        if(splitArrayClasses.length>2){
         backgroundCol = splitArrayClasses[2];
          if(backgroundCol.toLowerCase()=='red'){
            backgroundCol = "#e71b28";
          }
        }
        if(splitArrayClasses.length>3){
         tagName = splitArrayClasses[3];
        }
        if(splitArrayClasses.length>4){
         tagName = tagName+ " " +splitArrayClasses[4];
        }
        if(splitArrayClasses.length>5){
         tagName = tagName+ " " +splitArrayClasses[5];
        }
        var tagHTML = "<p class='labelHomepageStories' style='background-color:"+backgroundCol+";'>"+tagName+"</p>";
        if(storyPosition == "story1"){
          $('div.section-headlines div.leading-headline div.article-list').prepend(tagHTML);
        } else {
          var storyPositionRequired = storyPosition.substring(5) - 1;
          var checkTagline2 = $('div.section-headlines div.grid-articles-container div.first-row > div.article-grid-item:nth-child('+storyPositionRequired+') > div.article-link').find("div.article-text");
          $('div.section-headlines div.grid-articles-container div.first-row > div.article-grid-item:nth-child('+storyPositionRequired+') > div.article-link div.article-text').prepend(tagHTML);
        }
      }
    }
  });

     <script>
      $(window).load(loadFunction);$(window).resize(loadFunction);function loadFunction(a){setCarouselItemsWidth(calculateNumCarouselItems());setCarouselControlsHeight()}function setCarouselControlsHeight(){var a=$(".story-carousel"),b=$(".story-carousel .control"),c=b.outerHeight(),d=(a.outerHeight()-c)/2+"px";b.each(function(){$(this).css("margin-top",d);$(this).children("i").css("color","#fff")})}

$(function(){reorganisedCarousels||(reorganisedCarousels=!0,$(".story-carousel").each(function(a,b){var c=a*calculateNumCarouselItems();for(i=0;i<c;i++)$(this).find(".control-right").click()}))});

	if ($(window).width() < 767) {
		deskHBPAd.prependTo($deskHBPLocationDiv);
	}
});

   <script>
    function getOperatingSystem() {
  var userAgent = navigator.userAgent || navigator.vendor || window.opera;
    // iOS detection from: http://stackoverflow.com/a/9039885/177710
    if (/(Mac|iPad|iPhone|iPod)/.test(userAgent) && !window.MSStream) {
      userAgent = "iOS";
      return userAgent;
    } else {
      userAgent = "Android";
      return userAgent;
    }
}
   </script>
   <script>
    $(document).ready(function() {
  var ereaderURL="";
  var appURL="";
  var userAgentVal = getOperatingSystem();
  if (userAgentVal !="" && userAgentVal == "Android") {
    ereaderURL = "https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.newspaperdirect.thenationalandroid";
    appURL = "https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.the.national";
  }else if (userAgentVal !="" && userAgentVal == "iOS") {
    ereaderURL = "https://itunes.apple.com/us/app/the-national-e-reader/id522987896?mt=8";
    appURL = "https://itunes.apple.com/za/app/the-national-uae/id1281497691?mt=8";
  }
  if($("#e-reader-selector").length > 0 || ".e-reader-selector".length > 0) {
    $('#e-reader-selector').attr('href',ereaderURL);
    $('.e-reader-selector').attr('href',ereaderURL);
  }
  if($("#mob-app-selector").length > 0) {
    $('#mob-app-selector').attr('href',appURL);
  }
  var checkAPPLink = $('footer > div.sitemap > div.links-block:last-child > ul').find("li:nth-child(2)");
  if(checkAPPLink.length > 0){
    $('footer > div.sitemap > div.links-block:last-child > ul > li:nth-child(2) > a').attr('target',"_blank").attr('rel',"noreferrer").attr('href',appURL);
  }
});
   </script>

   <script>
    function onManageWebPushSubscriptionButtonClicked(event) {
     //console.log("onManageWebPushSubscriptionButtonClicked");
         getSubscriptionState().then(function(state) {
             if (state.isPushEnabled) {
                 /* Subscribed, opt them out */
                 OneSignal.setSubscription(false);
             } else {
                 if (state.isOptedOut) {
                     /* Opted out, opt them back in */
                     OneSignal.setSubscription(true);
                 } else {
                     /* Unsubscribed, subscribe them */
                     OneSignal.registerForPushNotifications();
                 }
             }
         });
         event.preventDefault();
     }
   
     function updateMangeWebPushSubscriptionButton(buttonSelector) {
       //console.log("updateMangeWebPushSubscriptionButton calld");
         var hideWhenSubscribed = false;
         var subscribeText = "Subscribe";
         var unsubscribeText = "Unsubscribe";
   
         getSubscriptionState().then(function(state) {
             var buttonText = !state.isPushEnabled || state.isOptedOut ? subscribeText : unsubscribeText;
   
             var element = document.querySelector(buttonSelector);
             
             if (element === null) {
                 return;
             }
   
             element.removeEventListener('click', onManageWebPushSubscriptionButtonClicked);
             element.addEventListener('click', onManageWebPushSubscriptionButtonClicked);
             element.textContent = buttonText;
           //console.log(element.textContent);
             
           if(element.textContent == "unsubscribe"){
             $("#opt-btn").text('Cancel');
             }
   
             if (state.hideWhenSubscribed && state.isPushEnabled) {
                 element.style.display = "none";
             } else {
                 element.style.display = "";
             }
         });
     }
   
     function getSubscriptionState() {
       //console.log("getSubscriptionState calld");
         return Promise.all([
           OneSignal.isPushNotificationsEnabled(),
           OneSignal.isOptedOut()
         ]).then(function(result) {
             var isPushEnabled = result[0];
             var isOptedOut = result[1];
   
             return {
                 isPushEnabled: isPushEnabled,
                 isOptedOut: isOptedOut
             };
         });
       
     }
   
     var OneSignal = OneSignal || [];
     var buttonSelector = "#my-notification-button";
   
     /* This example assumes you've already initialized OneSignal */
     OneSignal.push(function() {
         // If we're on an unsupported browser, do nothing
         if (!OneSignal.isPushNotificationsSupported()) {
             return;
         }
         updateMangeWebPushSubscriptionButton(buttonSelector);
         OneSignal.on("subscriptionChange", function(isSubscribed) {
             /* If the user's subscription state changes during the page's session, update the button text */
             updateMangeWebPushSubscriptionButton(buttonSelector);
           	 console.log("The user's subscription state is now:", isSubscribed);
              OneSignal.getUserId( function(userId) {
                ga('send', {
                  hitType: 'event',
                  eventCategory: 'Bell_Icon_subscribes',
                  eventAction: 'u_id ' + userId,
                  eventLabel: isSubscribed,
                  hitCallback: function() {
                  //console.log("ga os_subscriptionChange callback");
                  }
                });
              })
         });
     });
   </script>
  </div>
